msg:I came to Hengyang to play during the May Day holiday. Because this hotel was newly renovated and opened, I chose this one.
Environment: spacious space, smart toilet, high floor and very comfortable.
Hygiene: cleaned in time, very clean.
Facilities: There is a 24-hour laundry room for washing and drying, which is very convenient; there are many types of breakfast, and there are also special fish noodles and rice noodles, which are delicious~
One or two points of slight criticism are: First, because there is a roundabout overpass opposite, it will be a bit noisy. Second, the amount of fruit sent is a bit small, but it is quite delicious. Third, the most important point is that the poetic room type shown in the Ctrip picture does not match the actual landscape. According to the front desk staff, the picture was not taken by the hotel but by Ctrip. I wanted the scenery in the picture, but in fact there are two high-rise buildings opposite. I went up and down the stairs three times to change rooms. Fortunately, the staff was very patient and helped me choose and showed me the room type.
Overall, the accommodation experience is very good, clean and tidy, and the location is very convenient. It is recommended to experience it!

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Guestroom (Double Bed)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:2 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:Stayed here for 3 days during the Qingming Festival
Let me talk about the disadvantages first:
1. The air conditioning cooling logic is wrong. It must be turned on at 24 degrees to cool. Except for 24 degrees, it is heating. I woke up from the heat without covering the quilt for the first 2 nights. After the feedback on the third night, the room aunt brought me an electric fan
2. The air conditioning panel continues to glow, which really affects my sleep as a dark star, especially on the second night, when it was hot again, and the air conditioning panel was facing the bed, like a beam of light guiding my future life, illuminating me. I rolled on the bed for more than 2 hours and thought about my life. I usually sleep 8-9 hours at home, and I slept about 6 hours for the 3 nights I stayed here. (The way to deal with it, on the third night, let the aunt help to stick paper on the panel to block the glow)
Really, I strongly recommend that you communicate with the air conditioning designer, either the panel should not glow, or if the panel glows, don't face the bed, it's too uncomfortable for dark stars, and the air conditioning should be normal, and the wind will blow at a certain degree when the temperature is adjusted. Please

Advantages: New, the hotel is really new, and the decoration style is also very elegant. Excluding the air conditioning design of the logic genius, other facilities are quite good. The laundry room, gym, parking space, and restaurant are all in place.

The service is also good. When I was doing laundry, I told the auntie that I would check out at 11 o'clock on the last day. The auntie washed the clothes and delivered them directly to the room the next day.

There is a free midnight snack (1 serving) at night, and various convenience items are provided (sanitary napkins, makeup mirrors, lighters, etc.)

If the air conditioning is improved next year, I should still stay here next year, otherwise I will stay back at Atour. The sleep quality in these 3 days is really too bad

msg:Yijian Junya Hotel
The very modern design is implemented in every corner of the lobby, restaurant and room, which is very stylish. The most surprising thing is that the room has a built-in smart home robot called T. It can turn on and off the lights and curtains and ask for hotel services by just speaking a few commands. In addition, there is a QR code in the room where you can request to borrow facial creams, facial masks, etc. for free, as well as order late night snacks and hot drinks. After checking in at the front desk, they took us into the room and gave us an introduction. When we checked out, we were given fruits and water, as well as free umbrellas. A very luxurious and comfortable stay, highly recommended!

Hygiene: Because it is new, it will not be bad. There is scale on the kettle for boiling water. It is recommended to remove it regularly.
Environment: It takes about half an hour from the high-speed rail station to the hotel during off-peak hours. It is within walking distance from the city government. The traffic during peak hours is still quite urgent, so be careful with children. There is a gym and laundry room on the 26th floor.
Service: The front desk is very enthusiastic and the check-in is also very smooth. The first time I encountered a child checking in, I had to take a photo and upload it to the public security group for reporting. The room service is also very enthusiastic, but the response is a bit slow.
Food: The quality of breakfast is OK, but there are fewer varieties. The midnight snack is not bad.
